create or replace PROCEDURE "BRF204_MAPPING_PROCEDURE" (REPORT_DATE VARCHAR2) 

IS 

  V_REPORT_DATE DATE := To_date (REPORT_DATE, 'DD-MM-YYYY'); 

   V_FROM_DATE dATE :=  ADD_MONTHS (LAST_DAY (REPORT_DATE), -1) + 1;

BEGIN

--insert
insert into BRF204_MAPPING_TABLE
(foracid, cust_id, ACCT_NAME,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE,GL_CODE, SCHM_CODE,NRE_STATUS,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,REPORT_DATE,CONSTITUTION_CODE,ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,BACID,SOL_ID,LEGAL_ENTITY_TYPE,HNI_NETWORTH,TURNOVER,PURPOSE_OF_ADVN,country_of_incorp)
SELECT  ACCT_NUMBER,cust_id, ACCT_NAME,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE, GL_CODE,SCHM_CODE,NRE_FLG,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,REPORT_DATE,CONSTITUTION_CODE,ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,BACID,SOL_ID,LEGAL_ENTITY_TYPE,HNI_NETWORTH,TURNOVER,PURPOSE_OF_ADVN,country_of_incorp
FROM general_master_table WHERE report_date = '30-jun-2023';


insert into BRF204_MAPPING_TABLE
(FORACID, ACCT_NAME,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,REPORT_DATE,ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC)
SELECT  ACCT_NO,ACCT_NAME,CURRENCY,REPORT_DATE,AMT_LC
FROM BRF_TREASURY_MASTER_TB WHERE report_date = '30-jun-2023' AND ACCT_NO NOT IN  ('A31013016', 'A31031210', 'A34022024', 'A34022200', 'A66044200','A33012100');

INSERT INTO brf204_mapping_table(ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,ACCT_NAME,FORACID,NRE_STATUS,REPORT_DATE) 
SELECT 
ACCT_BALANCE_LC,
ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,
ACCT_NAME,
ACCT_NO,
NRE_FLG,
REPORT_DATE FROM brf_treasury_invest_tb WHERE brf_treasury_invest_tb.report_date='30-jun-2023';




--ROW107
UPDATE BRF204_MAPPING_TABLE SET  REPORT_NAME_1 ='BRF204', REPORT_LABEL_1 = 'ROW107' , report_addl_criteria_1 ='ROW107A'
WHERE   foracid IN ('A61111001','A61111002','A61111003','A61111004','A61150000')
AND COUNTRY_OF_INCORP IN ('SA')  AND 
ACCT_CRNCY_CODE IN ('AED') AND country_of_incorp not IN ('AE','AE*','UAE');
COMMIT;

UPDATE BRF204_MAPPING_TABLE SET  REPORT_NAME_1 ='BRF204', REPORT_LABEL_1 = 'ROW107' , report_addl_criteria_1 ='ROW107A'
WHERE gl_sub_head_code IN ('31104') AND  FORACID IN ('90010200012605','90010200012604','90010200018894') AND 
SOL_ID IN ('9001','9002','9003','9004','9005','9008')  
AND COUNTRY_OF_INCORP IN ('SA')AND ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC<0 and
ACCT_CRNCY_CODE IN ('AED')AND country_of_incorp not IN ('AE','AE*','UAE');
COMMIT;

----UPDATE BRF204_MAPPING_TABLE SET  REPORT_NAME_1 ='BRF204', REPORT_LABEL_1 = 'ROW176' , report_addl_criteria_1 ='ROW176L';
--
--COMMIT;



commit;
end;



--------


create or replace PROCEDURE BRF204_DETAIL_PROCEDURE (REPORT_DATE VARCHAR2)
 
IS
 
  V_REPORT_DATE DATE := To_date (REPORT_DATE, 'DD-MM-YYYY');

  -- V_FROM_DATE dATE :=  ADD_MONTHS (LAST_DAY (REPORT_DATE), -1) + 1;

BEGIN

delete from BRF204_DETAILTABLE where report_date = v_report_date;
commit;

insert into brf204_detailtable
(ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,ACCT_NAME,ACID,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,CUST_ID,FORACID,NRE_FLG,REMARKS,REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1,REPORT_DATE,REPORT_LABEL_1,REPORT_NAME_1,SOL_ID)
select ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,ACCT_NAME,ACID,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,CUST_ID,FORACID,NRE_STATUS,REMARKS,REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1,REPORT_DATE,REPORT_LABEL_1,REPORT_NAME_1,SOL_ID from brf204_mapping_table 
where report_date='30-jun-2023' and report_label_1 is not null;



COMMIT;
END;
